<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ivoor.html>ivoor</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ivoren.html>ivoren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ivoor.html>ivoortje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Pyxid_Al_Mughira_OA_4068.jpg/250px-Pyxid_Al_Mughira_OA_4068.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="379" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Pyxid_Al_Mughira_OA_4068.jpg/375px-Pyxid_Al_Mughira_OA_4068.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Pyxid_Al_Mughira_OA_4068.jpg/500px-Pyxid_Al_Mughira_OA_4068.jpg 2x" data-file-width="950" data-file-height="1440" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>Moorish ivory pyxis, 968 <small class="ce-date"><span title="Glossary and display preference">CE</span></small> (<a href = vnd.unilang:louvre.html>Louvre</a>)</div></div></div>

<li>an ivory <a href = vnd.unilang:artifact.html>artifact</a></li></ol>

***jaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> (163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jâer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">jār</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jērą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yeh₁-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaren.html>jaren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaartje.html>jaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>year</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The singular form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> normally in used after numerals and stock phrases instead of plurals but both are considered correct grammatically. Thus, it would be more common to say "<i><a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>vele</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaren.html>jaren</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geleden.html>geleden</a></i>" – many years ago; but "<i><a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geleden.html>geleden</a></i>" – "three years ago" or in "<i>in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>laatste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a></b></i>" as opposed to "<i>in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>laatste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaren.html>jaren</a></i>" ("in the last couple of years").
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jackass.html>jackass</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">jackasses</b>) 
</p>
<ol><li>a male donkey
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">fool</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">idiot</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dink.html>dink</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dope.html>dope</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">buffoon</span></span></dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">jerk</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">asshole</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">bastard</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a></span></span></dd></dl>

***jackpot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a> (11368)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Attested as <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">jack-pot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">big prize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, 1944; from sense "<a href = vnd.unilang:slot.html>slot</a> machine" (1932), from obsolete poker sense (1881) "antes that begin when no player <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a pair of <a href = vnd.unilang:jacks.html>jacks</a> or better"; from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">playing card</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpots.html>jackpots</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A money prize pool which accumulates until the conditions are <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> for it to be <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2000</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:daniel.html>Daniel</a> Kahneman and <a href = vnd.unilang:amos.html>Amos</a> Tversky,  <cite>Choices, values, and <a href = vnd.unilang:frames.html>frames</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">If no player picks all six numbers correctly, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> rolled <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> and added to the next week's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></b>; several weeks of rollovers can build up <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpots.html>jackpots</a></b> up to $350 million or more.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A large cash prize or money.</li>
<li>An unexpected windfall or reward.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">forestry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A concentration of surface wood or fuel.
<dl><dd><i>a juniper <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></b></i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>By metonymy, <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></b></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also the word for several <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a> of poker which feature <a href = vnd.unilang:jackpots.html>jackpots</a> (prize <a href = vnd.unilang:pools.html>pools</a> which accumulate until <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>).
<ul><li><b>1920</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/F._Scott_Fitzgerald" class="extiw" title="w:F. Scott Fitzgerald">F. Scott Fitzgerald</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/This_Side_of_Paradise/Book_One/Chapter_2" class="extiw" title="s:This Side of Paradise/Book One/Chapter 2">This Side of Paradise</a></i>,
<dl><dd>... they played red-dog and twenty-one and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></b> from dinner to dawn, and on the occasion of one <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>'s birthday persuaded him to buy sufficient <a href = vnd.unilang:champagne.html>champagne</a> for a hilarious celebration.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">hit the <a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpots.html>jackpots</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">jackpotting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">jackpotted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a <a href = vnd.unilang:slot.html>slot</a> machine<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To issue a <a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a>.
<ul><li><b>1999</b>, Martha Shirk, ‎J. Lawrence Aber, ‎Neil G. Bennett, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=wNIoAAAAYAAJamp;q=%22it+jackpotted%22amp;dq=%22it+jackpotted%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ved=0ahUKEwixgJHD_f7YAhUVS2MKHRX-ApEQ6AEIJzAA"><a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>Lives</a> on the Line: American <a href = vnd.unilang:families.html>Families</a> and the Struggle to Make <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>Ends</a> Meet</a>
<dl><dd>I <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> into the <a href = vnd.unilang:las.html>Las</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vegas.html>Vegas</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:casino.html>Casino</a> and played $20 in a nickel <a href = vnd.unilang:slot.html>slot</a>, and it <b>jackpotted</b> for $300.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2013</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amber_Dermont" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Amber Dermont"><a href = vnd.unilang:amber.html>Amber</a> Dermont</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=l_dj3wIhp50Camp;pg=PA96amp;dq=%22to+jackpot%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ved=0ahUKEwjL7NSt_P7YAhUJ3GMKHfhMDOs4FBDoAQgsMAEv=onepageamp;q=%22to%20jackpot%22amp;f=false">Damage Control: <a href = vnd.unilang:stories.html>Stories</a></a>

<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1912</b> June 18,  Supreme Court of Washington,  “HENDRICKSON v. SIMPSON LOGGING CO.”, in  <cite>The Pacific reporter‎</cite>, page 395:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It frequently <a href = vnd.unilang:happens.html>happens</a> that trees fall across one another, forming what <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> known as a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></b>. A number of trees may fall in a single <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></b>. One of the tools with which appellant claims a bucker should be provided <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an undercutter rigging. When trees are in a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></b>, the proper method of procedure <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to first cut the lower tree, and then the upper one. This lessens the liability of an upper log rolling or falling upon the workman while he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> engaged in cutting the lower tree. The cut of the lower tree <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ordinarily made by sawing it from the upper side, but, when its position produces a strain which pinches the saw, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sawed from the under side by what <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> known as an undercut. To make an undercut, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> necessary to have some appliance to support the moving saw which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> then operated teeth upward. The appliance which appellant contends <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> ordinarily used <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> known as an undercutter rigging. Having no undercutter rigging, appellant requested respondent's <a href = vnd.unilang:foreman.html>foreman</a> to provide one, complaining that his work in a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jackpot.html>jackpot</a></b> of large trees without one <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> unsafe and dangerous.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***jager.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jager.html>jager</a> (4390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:jager.html>jager</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">jageri</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jagen.html>jagen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jager.html>jager</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jagers.html>jagers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jagertje.html>jagertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">jaagster</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hunter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> destroyer <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">type of warship</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fighter, combat aeroplane
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jachtvliegtuig.html>jachtvliegtuig</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaeger.html>jaeger</a>, light infantry rifleman, ranger</li></ol>

***jaguar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a> (11871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Apparently borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tupi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tupi language">Old Tupi</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tpw">îagûara</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 1 | </a></sup> The contemporary pronunciation derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguars.html>jaguars</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></span> <span class="defdate">[from late 18th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1777</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Buffon, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> algemeene <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> byzondere natuurlyke <a href = vnd.unilang:historie.html>historie</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 5, part 1, tr. from French, J. H. Schneider (publ.), page 5.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:puma.html>puma</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> den <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:betreft.html>betreft</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> blykt duidelyk <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> beſchryvingen <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dieren.html>dieren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezien.html>gezien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:puma.html>puma</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leeuw.html>leeuw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> tyger; <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">As for the <a href = vnd.unilang:puma.html>puma</a> and the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></b>, it clearly appears from the descriptions by them, who have seen these animals, that the cougar <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not a lion, and [that] the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not a tiger; <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***jajem.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jajem.html>jajem</a> (82456)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">יין</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yayin</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">יַיִן</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yáyin</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<dl><dd>He wants to fight against high prices and for <b>servings of <a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></b> for five <a href = vnd.unilang:cents.html>cents</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***jak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jak.html>jak</a> (39389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Tibetan" class="extiw" title="w:Standard Tibetan">Tibetan</a></span> <i class="Tibt mention" lang="bo">གཡག</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bo-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">g.yag</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sino-Tibetan_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Sino-Tibetan languages">Proto-Sino-Tibetan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sit-pro">*g-jak ~ g-jaŋ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jak.html>jak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaks.html>jaks</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jak.html>jakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:yak.html>yak</a>, the ox-like Himalayan bovine, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bos.html>Bos</a> grunniens</i></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>(produce) <span class="Latn" lang="nl">jakboter</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">jakmelk</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">jacket</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jak.html>jak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jak.html>jakken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jak.html>jakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tight upper body garment</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jakhals.html>jakhals</a> (18225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from another European language, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">çakal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">شغال</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šağâl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">सृगाल</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sṛgālá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:jackal.html>jackal</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Modified into the current form by folk etymology.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jakhals.html>jakhals</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jakhalzen.html>jakhalzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jakhals.html>jakhalsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:jackal.html>jackal</a>, one of certain canids of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:canis.html>Canis</a></i>.</li></ol>
